UPDATE in_goodsrequest set module=0 WHERE module IS NULL;

CREATE TABLE `state` (
  `id` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `statename` varchar(200), 
  `statecode` varchar(32) DEFAULT NULL,
  `country` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (`country`) REFERENCES `country` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#Vipin Gupta 16 Mar, 2016
ALTER TABLE `locationbatchdocumentmapping` DROP FOREIGN KEY `locationbatchmapping_batchmapid`;
ALTER TABLE `locationbatchdocumentmapping` ADD CONSTRAINT `locationbatchmapping_batchmapid` FOREIGN KEY (`batchmapid`) REFERENCES `newproductbatch` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION;
ALTER TABLE `serialdocumentmapping` DROP FOREIGN KEY `serialdocumentmapping_serialmappid`;
ALTER TABLE `serialdocumentmapping` ADD CONSTRAINT `serialdocumentmapping_serialmappid` FOREIGN KEY (`serialid`) REFERENCES `newbatchserial` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION;
ALTER TABLE `newbatchserial` DROP FOREIGN KEY `batchSerialMapping_batch`;
ALTER TABLE `newbatchserial` ADD CONSTRAINT `batchSerialMapping_batch` FOREIGN KEY (`batch`) REFERENCES `newproductbatch` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE;

ALTER TABLE extracompanypreferences ADD gstdeactivationdate  date NULL;

CREATE TABLE gstformgenerationhistory (
    id varchar(255) NOT NULL,
    generationdate varchar(255),
    startdate varchar(255),
    enddate varchar(255),
    user varchar(255) NOT NULL,
    company varchar(255) NOT NULL,
    filename varchar(80),
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_gstformgenerationhistory_company` FOREIGN KEY (`company`) REFERENCES `company` (`companyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_gstformgenerationhistory_user` FOREIGN KEY (`user`) REFERENCES `users` (`userid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8 ;

#Neeraj Dwivedi 29th March 2016
CREATE TABLE `taxperiod` (
  `id` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `periodname` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `company` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
   startdate date,
   enddate date,
  `subperiodof` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `periodtype`  int(4) DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY  (`id`),
  FOREIGN KEY (company) REFERENCES company(companyid),
  FOREIGN KEY (subperiodof) REFERENCES taxperiod(id)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

# Nitesh Kumar 29 March 2016
CREATE TABLE `customreports` (
  `reportno` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `reportname` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `reportuniquename` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `summaryflag` char(1) DEFAULT 'T',
  `createdon` bigint(25) DEFAULT NULL,
  `createdbyid` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `updatedbyid` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `deleteflag` tinyint(4) DEFAULT NULL,
  `reportmodulecategory` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL,
  `reportmodule` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL,
  `reportjson` text,
  `groupflag` char(1) DEFAULT 'F',
  `reportsql` text,
  `reportdescription` varchar(1024) DEFAULT NULL,
  `updatedon` bigint(25) DEFAULT NULL,
  `companyid` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`reportno`),
  KEY `fk_customreports_1_idx` (`createdbyid`),
  KEY `updatedbyid` (`updatedbyid`),
  CONSTRAINT `customreports_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`createdbyid`) REFERENCES `users` (`userid`),
  CONSTRAINT `customreports_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`updatedbyid`) REFERENCES `users` (`userid`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=1 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

ALTER TABLE discount ADD COLUMN typeoffigure int(1) DEFAULT 0;
ALTER TABLE discount ADD COLUMN typefigure double DEFAULT 0;

update discount set typefigure = discount where typeoffigure = 1;
